```cpp
    setParameter("band" + std::to_string(band) + "_gain", m_bands[band].gain);
    updateBandFilter(band);
}

float Equalizer::getBandGain(int band) const {
    if (band < 0 || band >= m_numBands) return 0.0f;
    return m_bands[band].gain;
}

void Equalizer::setBandFrequency(int band, float frequency) {
    if (band < 0 || band >= m_numBands) return;
    
    m_bands[band].frequency = std::clamp(frequency, 20.0f, 20000.0f);
    setParameter("band" + std::to_string(band) + "_freq", m_bands[band].frequency);
    updateBandFilter(band);
}

float Equalizer::getBandFrequency(int band) const {
    if (band < 0 || band >= m_numBands) return 1000.0f;
    return m_bands[band].frequency;
}

void Equalizer::setBandQ(int band, float Q) {
    if (band < 0 || band >= m_numBands) return;
    
    m_bands[band].Q = std::clamp(Q, 0.1f, 10.0f);
    setParameter("band" + std::to_string(band) + "_q", m_bands[band].Q);
    updateBandFilter(band);
}

void Equalizer::setBandEnabled(int band, bool enabled) {
    if (band < 0 || band >= m_numBands) return;
    m_bands[band].enabled = enabled;
}

void Equalizer::setFlat() {
    for (int b = 0; b < m_numBands; ++b) {
        setBandGain(b, 0.0f);
    }
}

void Equalizer::setBassBoost() {
    if (m_numBands >= 10) {
        setBandGain(0, 8.0f);
        setBandGain(1, 6.0f);
        setBandGain(2, 4.0f);
        setBandGain(3, 2.0f);
        for (int b = 4; b < m_numBands; ++b) {
            setBandGain(b, 0.0f);
        }
    }
}

void Equalizer::setTrebleBoost() {
    if (m_numBands >= 10) {
        for (int b = 0; b < 5; ++b) {
            setBandGain(b, 0.0f);
        }
        setBandGain(5, 2.0f);
        setBandGain(6, 4.0f);
        setBandGain(7, 6.0f);
        setBandGain(8, 8.0f);
        setBandGain(9, 8.0f);
    }
}

void Equalizer::setVShape() {
    if (m_numBands >= 10) {
        std::array<float, 10> gains = {6, 4, 2, -2, -4, -4, -2, 2, 4, 6};
        for (int b = 0; b < 10; ++b) {
            setBandGain(b, gains[b]);
        }
    }
}

void Equalizer::setVocalBoost() {
    if (m_numBands >= 10) {
        std::array<float, 10> gains = {-2, -1, 0, 2, 4, 4, 2, 0, -1, -2};
        for (int b = 0; b < 10; ++b) {
            setBandGain(b, gains[b]);
        }
    }
}

std::vector<float> Equalizer::getFrequencyResponse(int numPoints) const {
    std::vector<float> response(numPoints);
    
    float minFreq = 20.0f;
    float maxFreq = 20000.0f;
    float logMin = std::log10(minFreq);
    float logMax = std::log10(maxFreq);
    
    for (int i = 0; i < numPoints; ++i) {
        float logFreq = logMin + (logMax - logMin) * i / (numPoints - 1);
        float freq = std::pow(10.0f, logFreq);
        response[i] = calculateFilterResponse(freq);
    }
    
    return response;
}

float Equalizer::calculateFilterResponse(float frequency) const {
    float totalGain = 0.0f;
    
    for (int b = 0; b < m_numBands; ++b) {
        if (!m_bands[b].enabled) continue;
        
        const auto& band = m_bands[b];
        const auto& coeffs = m_filters[b][0].getCoefficients();
        
        // Calculate frequency response of this biquad
        float w = 2.0f * M_PI * frequency / m_sampleRate;
        std::complex<float> z(std::cos(w), std::sin(w));
        std::complex<float> z2 = z * z;
        
        std::complex<float> num = coeffs.b0 + coeffs.b1 / z + coeffs.b2 / z2;
        std::complex<float> den = 1.0f + coeffs.a1 / z + coeffs.a2 / z2;
        
        float magnitude = std::abs(num / den);
        totalGain += 20.0f * std::log10(magnitude);
    }
    
    return totalGain;
}

EQBand& Equalizer::getBand(int index) {
    return m_bands[std::clamp(index, 0, m_numBands - 1)];
}

const EQBand& Equalizer::getBand(int index) const {
    return m_bands[std::clamp(index, 0, m_numBands - 1)];
}

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

## Compressor Implementation

```cpp
// src/core/effects/Compressor.hpp
#pragma once

#include "EffectBase.hpp"
#include <vector>
#include <atomic>

namespace SoundBoost {

class Compressor : public EffectBase {
public:
    Compressor();
    ~Compressor() override = default;
    
    void initialize(int sampleRate, int bufferSize) override;
    void process(AudioBuffer& buffer) override;
    void reset() override;
    
    std::string getName() const override { return "Compressor"; }
    std::string getCategory() const override { return "Dynamics"; }
    
    // Parameters
    void setThreshold(float thresholdDb);
    float getThreshold() const { return m_threshold; }
    
    void setRatio(float ratio);
    float getRatio() const { return m_ratio; }
    
    void setAttack(float attackMs);
    float getAttack() const { return m_attack; }
    
    void setRelease(float releaseMs);
    float getRelease() const { return m_release; }
    
    void setKnee(float kneeDb);
    float getKnee() const { return m_knee; }
    
    void setMakeupGain(float gainDb);
    float getMakeupGain() const { return m_makeupGain; }
    
    void setAutoMakeup(bool enabled);
    bool isAutoMakeup() const { return m_autoMakeup; }
    
    void setLookahead(float lookaheadMs);
    float getLookahead() const { return m_lookahead; }
    
    void setSidechain(bool enabled);
    bool isSidechainEnabled() const { return m_sidechainEnabled; }
    
    // Metering
    float getGainReduction() const { return m_currentGainReduction.load(); }
    float getInputLevel() const { return m_inputLevel.load(); }
    float getOutputLevel() const { return m_outputLevel.load(); }
    
private:
    void updateCoefficients();
    float computeGain(float inputLevel);
    float softKnee(float inputDb, float thresholdDb, float kneeDb, float ratio);
    
    // Parameters
    float m_threshold{-20.0f};      // dB
    float m_ratio{4.0f};            // :1
    float m_attack{10.0f};          // ms
    float m_release{100.0f};        // ms
    float m_knee{6.0f};             // dB
    float m_makeupGain{0.0f};       // dB
    float m_lookahead{0.0f};        // ms
    bool m_autoMakeup{false};
    bool m_sidechainEnabled{false};
    
    // Coefficients
    float m_attackCoeff{0.0f};
    float m_releaseCoeff{0.0f};
    float m_makeupLinear{1.0f};
    
    // State
    float m_envelope{0.0f};
    std::vector<float> m_lookaheadBuffer;
    size_t m_lookaheadWritePos{0};
    size_t m_lookaheadSamples{0};
    
    // Metering
    std::atomic<float> m_currentGainReduction{0.0f};
    std::atomic<float> m_inputLevel{0.0f};
    std::atomic<float> m_outputLevel{0.0f};
    
    int m_sampleRate{48000};
};

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

```cpp
// src/core/effects/Compressor.cpp
#include "Compressor.hpp"
#include "../../utils/MathUtils.hpp"

#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

namespace SoundBoost {

Compressor::Compressor() {
    registerParameter("threshold", -20.0f, -60.0f, 0.0f, "dB");
    registerParameter("ratio", 4.0f, 1.0f, 20.0f, ":1");
    registerParameter("attack", 10.0f, 0.1f, 100.0f, "ms");
    registerParameter("release", 100.0f, 10.0f, 1000.0f, "ms");
    registerParameter("knee", 6.0f, 0.0f, 24.0f, "dB");
    registerParameter("makeup", 0.0f, 0.0f, 24.0f, "dB");
}

void Compressor::initialize(int sampleRate, int bufferSize) {
    m_sampleRate = sampleRate;
    
    // Initialize lookahead buffer (max 10ms)
    size_t maxLookahead = static_cast<size_t>(0.01f * sampleRate * 2); // stereo
    m_lookaheadBuffer.resize(maxLookahead, 0.0f);
    m_lookaheadWritePos = 0;
    
    updateCoefficients();
    m_initialized = true;
}

void Compressor::updateCoefficients() {
    // Attack and release coefficients
    m_attackCoeff = std::exp(-1.0f / (m_attack * 0.001f * m_sampleRate));
    m_releaseCoeff = std::exp(-1.0f / (m_release * 0.001f * m_sampleRate));
    
    // Lookahead samples
    m_lookaheadSamples = static_cast<size_t>(m_lookahead * 0.001f * m_sampleRate);
    
    // Makeup gain
    if (m_autoMakeup) {
        // Estimate average gain reduction
        float avgReduction = (m_threshold * (1.0f - 1.0f / m_ratio)) / 2.0f;
        m_makeupLinear = std::pow(10.0f, -avgReduction / 20.0f);
    } else {
        m_makeupLinear = std::pow(10.0f, m_makeupGain / 20.0f);
    }
}

float Compressor::softKnee(float inputDb, float thresholdDb, float kneeDb, float ratio) {
    float halfKnee = kneeDb / 2.0f;
    
    if (inputDb < thresholdDb - halfKnee) {
        // Below knee
        return inputDb;
    } else if (inputDb > thresholdDb + halfKnee) {
        // Above knee
        return thresholdDb + (inputDb - thresholdDb) / ratio;
    } else {
        // In knee region - smooth transition
        float x = inputDb - thresholdDb + halfKnee;
        float compressionCurve = (1.0f / ratio - 1.0f) / (2.0f * kneeDb);
        return inputDb + compressionCurve * x * x;
    }
}

float Compressor::computeGain(float inputLevel) {
    // Convert to dB
    float inputDb = (inputLevel > 1e-10f) ? 20.0f * std::log10(inputLevel) : -100.0f;
    
    // Apply compression curve
    float outputDb;
    if (m_knee > 0.0f) {
        outputDb = softKnee(inputDb, m_threshold, m_knee, m_ratio);
    } else {
        // Hard knee
        if (inputDb > m_threshold) {
            outputDb = m_threshold + (inputDb - m_threshold) / m_ratio;
        } else {
            outputDb = inputDb;
        }
    }
    
    // Calculate gain reduction
    float gainReductionDb = outputDb - inputDb;
    return std::pow(10.0f, gainReductionDb / 20.0f);
}

void Compressor::process(AudioBuffer& buffer) {
    if (!m_enabled || !m_initialized) return;
    
    float* data = buffer.getData();
    size_t numSamples = buffer.getNumSamples();
    int channels = buffer.getNumChannels();
    
    float maxInputLevel = 0.0f;
    float maxOutputLevel = 0.0f;
    float maxGainReduction = 0.0f;
    
    for (size_t i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
        // Calculate input level (max of all channels)
        float inputLevel = 0.0f;
        for (int ch = 0; ch < channels; ++ch) {
            inputLevel = std::max(inputLevel, std::abs(data[i * channels + ch]));
        }
        maxInputLevel = std::max(maxInputLevel, inputLevel);
        
        // Envelope follower (peak detection)
        float targetEnv = inputLevel;
        if (targetEnv > m_envelope) {
            m_envelope = m_attackCoeff * m_envelope + (1.0f - m_attackCoeff) * targetEnv;
        } else {
            m_envelope = m_releaseCoeff * m_envelope + (1.0f - m_releaseCoeff) * targetEnv;
        }
        
        // Compute gain
        float gain = computeGain(m_envelope);
        
        // Apply makeup gain
        gain *= m_makeupLinear;
        
        // Track gain reduction
        float gr = 1.0f - gain / m_makeupLinear;
        maxGainReduction = std::max(maxGainReduction, gr);
        
        // Apply gain to all channels
        for (int ch = 0; ch < channels; ++ch) {
            size_t idx = i * channels + ch;
            data[idx] *= gain;
            maxOutputLevel = std::max(maxOutputLevel, std::abs(data[idx]));
        }
    }
    
    // Update meters
    m_inputLevel.store(maxInputLevel);
    m_outputLevel.store(maxOutputLevel);
    m_currentGainReduction.store(maxGainReduction);
}

void Compressor::reset() {
    m_envelope = 0.0f;
    std::fill(m_lookaheadBuffer.begin(), m_lookaheadBuffer.end(), 0.0f);
    m_lookaheadWritePos = 0;
    m_currentGainReduction.store(0.0f);
    m_inputLevel.store(0.0f);
    m_outputLevel.store(0.0f);
}

void Compressor::setThreshold(float thresholdDb) {
    m_threshold = std::clamp(thresholdDb, -60.0f, 0.0f);
    setParameter("threshold", m_threshold);
    updateCoefficients();
}

void Compressor::setRatio(float ratio) {
    m_ratio = std::clamp(ratio, 1.0f, 20.0f);
    setParameter("ratio", m_ratio);
    updateCoefficients();
}

void Compressor::setAttack(float attackMs) {
    m_attack = std::clamp(attackMs, 0.1f, 100.0f);
    setParameter("attack", m_attack);
    updateCoefficients();
}

void Compressor::setRelease(float releaseMs) {
    m_release = std::clamp(releaseMs, 10.0f, 1000.0f);
    setParameter("release", m_release);
    updateCoefficients();
}

void Compressor::setKnee(float kneeDb) {
    m_knee = std::clamp(kneeDb, 0.0f, 24.0f);
    setParameter("knee", m_knee);
}

void Compressor::setMakeupGain(float gainDb) {
    m_makeupGain = std::clamp(gainDb, 0.0f, 24.0f);
    setParameter("makeup", m_makeupGain);
    updateCoefficients();
}

void Compressor::setAutoMakeup(bool enabled) {
    m_autoMakeup = enabled;
    updateCoefficients();
}

void Compressor::setLookahead(float lookaheadMs) {
    m_lookahead = std::clamp(lookaheadMs, 0.0f, 10.0f);
    updateCoefficients();
}

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

## Limiter Implementation

```cpp
// src/core/effects/Limiter.hpp
#pragma once

#include "EffectBase.hpp"
#include <vector>
#include <atomic>

namespace SoundBoost {

class Limiter : public EffectBase {
public:
    Limiter();
    ~Limiter() override = default;
    
    void initialize(int sampleRate, int bufferSize) override;
    void process(AudioBuffer& buffer) override;
    void reset() override;
    
    std::string getName() const override { return "Limiter"; }
    std::string getCategory() const override { return "Dynamics"; }
    
    // Parameters
    void setCeiling(float ceilingDb);
    float getCeiling() const { return m_ceiling; }
    
    void setRelease(float releaseMs);
    float getRelease() const { return m_release; }
    
    void setLookahead(float lookaheadMs);
    float getLookahead() const { return m_lookahead; }
    
    void setTruePeak(bool enabled);
    bool isTruePeak() const { return m_truePeak; }
    
    // Metering
    float getGainReduction() const { return m_gainReduction.load(); }
    
private:
    void updateCoefficients();
    float interpolateSample(const float* buffer, float position, size_t bufferSize);
    float findTruePeak(const float* samples, size_t count);
    
    float m_ceiling{-0.3f};       // dB
    float m_release{50.0f};       // ms
    float m_lookahead{1.0f};      // ms
    bool m_truePeak{true};
    
    float m_ceilingLinear{1.0f};
    float m_releaseCoeff{0.0f};
    size_t m_lookaheadSamples{0};
    
    std::vector<std::vector<float>> m_lookaheadBuffer;
    size_t m_lookaheadWritePos{0};
    
    float m_currentGain{1.0f};
    std::atomic<float> m_gainReduction{0.0f};
    
    int m_sampleRate{48000};
    int m_numChannels{2};
};

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

```cpp
// src/core/effects/Limiter.cpp
#include "Limiter.hpp"
#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

namespace SoundBoost {

Limiter::Limiter() {
    registerParameter("ceiling", -0.3f, -12.0f, 0.0f, "dB");
    registerParameter("release", 50.0f, 1.0f, 500.0f, "ms");
    registerParameter("lookahead", 1.0f, 0.0f, 5.0f, "ms");
}

void Limiter::initialize(int sampleRate, int bufferSize) {
    m_sampleRate = sampleRate;
    m_numChannels = 2;
    
    // Lookahead buffer (5ms max)
    size_t maxLookahead = static_cast<size_t>(0.005f * sampleRate);
    m_lookaheadBuffer.resize(m_numChannels);
    for (auto& buf : m_lookaheadBuffer) {
        buf.resize(maxLookahead, 0.0f);
    }
    m_lookaheadWritePos = 0;
    
    updateCoefficients();
    m_initialized = true;
}

void Limiter::updateCoefficients() {
    m_ceilingLinear = std::pow(10.0f, m_ceiling / 20.0f);
    m_releaseCoeff = std::exp(-1.0f / (m_release * 0.001f * m_sampleRate));
    m_lookaheadSamples = static_cast<size_t>(m_lookahead * 0.001f * m_sampleRate);
}

float Limiter::findTruePeak(const float* samples, size_t count) {
    float maxPeak = 0.0f;
    
    // 4x oversampling for true peak detection
    for (size_t i = 0; i < count - 1; ++i) {
        float s0 = samples[i];
        float s1 = samples[i + 1];
        
        // Find peak in interpolated samples
        for (int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {
            float t = j / 4.0f;
            // Simple linear interpolation (could use sinc for better accuracy)
            float interp = s0 + (s1 - s0) * t;
            maxPeak = std::max(maxPeak, std::abs(interp));
        }
    }
    
    return maxPeak;
}

void Limiter::process(AudioBuffer& buffer) {
    if (!m_enabled || !m_initialized) return;
    
    float* data = buffer.getData();
    size_t numSamples = buffer.getNumSamples();
    int channels = buffer.getNumChannels();
    
    // Adjust buffers if channels changed
    if (channels != m_numChannels) {
        m_numChannels = channels;
        size_t bufSize = m_lookaheadBuffer[0].size();
        m_lookaheadBuffer.resize(channels);
        for (auto& buf : m_lookaheadBuffer) {
            buf.resize(bufSize, 0.0f);
        }
    }
    
    float maxGR = 0.0f;
    
    for (size_t i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
        // Find peak across all channels
        float peak = 0.0f;
        for (int ch = 0; ch < channels; ++ch) {
            peak = std::max(peak, std::abs(data[i * channels + ch]));
        }
        
        // True peak detection
        if (m_truePeak && i > 0) {
            // Check interpolated samples
            for (int ch = 0; ch < channels; ++ch) {
                float prev = data[(i - 1) * channels + ch];
                float curr = data[i * channels + ch];
                float interPeak = std::max(std::abs(prev), std::abs(curr));
                // Estimate interpolated peak
                float midpoint = std::abs((prev + curr) / 2.0f);
                interPeak = std::max(interPeak, midpoint * 1.1f); // Approximation
                peak = std::max(peak, interPeak);
            }
        }
        
        // Calculate required gain
        float targetGain = 1.0f;
        if (peak > m_ceilingLinear) {
            targetGain = m_ceilingLinear / peak;
        }
        
        // Smooth gain changes
        if (targetGain < m_currentGain) {
            // Instant attack for limiting
            m_currentGain = targetGain;
        } else {
            // Smooth release
            m_currentGain = m_releaseCoeff * m_currentGain + (1.0f - m_releaseCoeff) * targetGain;
        }
        
        // Track gain reduction
        float gr = 1.0f - m_currentGain;
        maxGR = std::max(maxGR, gr);
        
        // Apply gain
        for (int ch = 0; ch < channels; ++ch) {
            size_t idx = i * channels + ch;
            data[idx] *= m_currentGain;
            
            // Hard clip as safety (should rarely trigger)
            data[idx] = std::clamp(data[idx], -m_ceilingLinear, m_ceilingLinear);
        }
    }
    
    m_gainReduction.store(maxGR);
}

void Limiter::reset() {
    m_currentGain = 1.0f;
    for (auto& buf : m_lookaheadBuffer) {
        std::fill(buf.begin(), buf.end(), 0.0f);
    }
    m_lookaheadWritePos = 0;
    m_gainReduction.store(0.0f);
}

void Limiter::setCeiling(float ceilingDb) {
    m_ceiling = std::clamp(ceilingDb, -12.0f, 0.0f);
    setParameter("ceiling", m_ceiling);
    updateCoefficients();
}

void Limiter::setRelease(float releaseMs) {
    m_release = std::clamp(releaseMs, 1.0f, 500.0f);
    setParameter("release", m_release);
    updateCoefficients();
}

void Limiter::setLookahead(float lookaheadMs) {
    m_lookahead = std::clamp(lookaheadMs, 0.0f, 5.0f);
    setParameter("lookahead", m_lookahead);
    updateCoefficients();
}

void Limiter::setTruePeak(bool enabled) {
    m_truePeak = enabled;
}

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

## Stereo Widener Implementation

```cpp
// src/core/effects/StereoWidener.hpp
#pragma once

#include "EffectBase.hpp"
#include "../dsp/BiquadFilter.hpp"
#include <vector>

namespace SoundBoost {

class StereoWidener : public EffectBase {
public:
    StereoWidener();
    ~StereoWidener() override = default;
    
    void initialize(int sampleRate, int bufferSize) override;
    void process(AudioBuffer& buffer) override;
    void reset() override;
    
    std::string getName() const override { return "Stereo Widener"; }
    std::string getCategory() const override { return "Spatial"; }
    
    // Parameters
    void setWidth(float width);  // 0-200%, 100% = normal
    float getWidth() const { return m_width; }
    
    void setMidGain(float gainDb);
    float getMidGain() const { return m_midGain; }
    
    void setSideGain(float gainDb);
    float getSideGain() const { return m_sideGain; }
    
    void setBassMono(bool enabled);
    bool isBassMono() const { return m_bassMono; }
    
    void setBassMonoFreq(float frequency);
    float getBassMonoFreq() const { return m_bassMonoFreq; }
    
    void setDelay(float delayMs);  // Haas effect
    float getDelay() const { return m_delay; }
    
private:
    void updateFilters();
    
    float m_width{100.0f};        // Percentage
    float m_midGain{0.0f};        // dB
    float m_sideGain{0.0f};       // dB
    bool m_bassMono{true};
    float m_bassMonoFreq{200.0f}; // Hz
    float m_delay{0.0f};          // ms
    
    // Filters for bass mono
    BiquadFilter m_lowPassL;
    BiquadFilter m_lowPassR;
    BiquadFilter m_highPassL;
    BiquadFilter m_highPassR;
    
    // Delay buffer for Haas effect
    std::vector<float> m_delayBuffer;
    size_t m_delayWritePos{0};
    size_t m_delaySamples{0};
    
    int m_sampleRate{48000};
};

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

```cpp
// src/core/effects/StereoWidener.cpp
#include "StereoWidener.hpp"
#include "../dsp/FilterDesign.hpp"

#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

namespace SoundBoost {

StereoWidener::StereoWidener() {
    registerParameter("width", 100.0f, 0.0f, 200.0f, "%");
    registerParameter("mid_gain", 0.0f, -12.0f, 12.0f, "dB");
    registerParameter("side_gain", 0.0f, -12.0f, 12.0f, "dB");
    registerParameter("bass_mono_freq", 200.0f, 50.0f, 500.0f, "Hz");
    registerParameter("delay", 0.0f, 0.0f, 30.0f, "ms");
}

void StereoWidener::initialize(int sampleRate, int bufferSize) {
    m_sampleRate = sampleRate;
    
    // Delay buffer (max 30ms)
    size_t maxDelaySamples = static_cast<size_t>(0.03f * sampleRate);
    m_delayBuffer.resize(maxDelaySamples, 0.0f);
    m_delayWritePos = 0;
    
    updateFilters();
    m_initialized = true;
}

void StereoWidener::updateFilters() {
    auto lpCoeffs = FilterDesign::lowPass(m_sampleRate, m_bassMonoFreq, 0.707f);
    auto hpCoeffs = FilterDesign::highPass(m_sampleRate, m_bassMonoFreq, 0.707f);
    
    m_lowPassL.setCoefficients(lpCoeffs);
    m_lowPassR.setCoefficients(lpCoeffs);
    m_highPassL.setCoefficients(hpCoeffs);
    m_highPassR.setCoefficients(hpCoeffs);
    
    m_delaySamples = static_cast<size_t>(m_delay * 0.001f * m_sampleRate);
}

void StereoWidener::process(AudioBuffer& buffer) {
    if (!m_enabled || !m_initialized) return;
    if (buffer.getNumChannels() < 2) return; // Need stereo
    
    float* data = buffer.getData();
    size_t numSamples = buffer.getNumSamples();
    int channels = buffer.getNumChannels();
    
    float widthCoeff = m_width / 100.0f;
    float midCoeff = std::pow(10.0f, m_midGain / 20.0f);
    float sideCoeff = std::pow(10.0f, m_sideGain / 20.0f) * widthCoeff;
    
    for (size_t i = 0; i < numSamples; ++i) {
        float left = data[i * channels];
        float right = data[i * channels + 1];
        
        // Apply Haas effect delay to one channel
        float delayedRight = right;
        if (m_delaySamples > 0) {
            // Read from delay buffer
            size_t readPos = (m_delayWritePos + m_delayBuffer.size() - m_delaySamples) 
                            % m_delayBuffer.size();
            delayedRight = m_delayBuffer[readPos];
            
            // Write to delay buffer
            m_delayBuffer[m_delayWritePos] = right;
            m_delayWritePos = (m_delayWritePos + 1) % m_delayBuffer.size();
        }
        
        if (m_bassMono) {
            // Split into low and high frequency
            float lowL = m_lowPassL.process(left);
            float lowR = m_lowPassR.process(delayedRight);
            float highL = m_highPassL.process(left);
            float highR = m_highPassR.process(delayedRight);
            
            // Make bass mono
            float monoLow = (lowL + lowR) * 0.5f;
            
            // Apply M/S processing to high frequencies only
            float mid = (highL + highR) * 0.5f;
            float side = (highL - highR) * 0.5f;
            
            // Apply gains
            mid *= midCoeff;
            side *= sideCoeff;
            
            // Convert back to L/R
            highL = mid + side;
            highR = mid - side;
            
            // Combine
            left = monoLow + highL;
            right = monoLow + highR;
        } else {
            // Standard M/S processing
            float mid = (left + delayedRight) * 0.5f;
            float side = (left - delayedRight) * 0.5f;
            
            // Apply gains
            mid *= midCoeff;
            side *= sideCoeff;
            
            // Convert back to L/R
            left = mid + side;
            right = mid - side;
        }
        
        data[i * channels] = left;
        data[i * channels + 1] = right;
    }
}

void StereoWidener::reset() {
    m_lowPassL.reset();
    m_lowPassR.reset();
    m_highPassL.reset();
    m_highPassR.reset();
    std::fill(m_delayBuffer.begin(), m_delayBuffer.end(), 0.0f);
    m_delayWritePos = 0;
}

void StereoWidener::setWidth(float width) {
    m_width = std::clamp(width, 0.0f, 200.0f);
    setParameter("width", m_width);
}

void StereoWidener::setMidGain(float gainDb) {
    m_midGain = std::clamp(gainDb, -12.0f, 12.0f);
    setParameter("mid_gain", m_midGain);
}

void StereoWidener::setSideGain(float gainDb) {
    m_sideGain = std::clamp(gainDb, -12.0f, 12.0f);
    setParameter("side_gain", m_sideGain);
}

void StereoWidener::setBassMono(bool enabled) {
    m_bassMono = enabled;
}

void StereoWidener::setBassMonoFreq(float frequency) {
    m_bassMonoFreq = std::clamp(frequency, 50.0f, 500.0f);
    setParameter("bass_mono_freq", m_bassMonoFreq);
    updateFilters();
}

void StereoWidener::setDelay(float delayMs) {
    m_delay = std::clamp(delayMs, 0.0f, 30.0f);
    setParameter("delay", m_delay);
    m_delaySamples = static_cast<size_t>(m_delay * 0.001f * m_sampleRate);
}

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

## Windows WASAPI Audio Capture

```cpp
// src/platform/windows/WASAPICapture.hpp
#pragma once

#ifdef PLATFORM_WINDOWS

#include "../AudioCaptureBase.hpp"
#include <windows.h>
#include <mmdeviceapi.h>
#include <audioclient.h>
#include <functiondiscoverykeys_devpkey.h>

#include <thread>
#include <atomic>
#include <mutex>
#include <memory>

namespace SoundBoost {

class WASAPICapture : public AudioCaptureBase {
public:
    WASAPICapture();
    ~WASAPICapture() override;
    
    bool initialize(int sampleRate, int bufferSize, int channels) override;
    void start() override;
    void stop() override;
    bool isRunning() const override { return m_running.load(); }
    
    std::vector<AudioDevice> getAvailableDevices() override;
    bool setDevice(const std::string& deviceId) override;
    std::string getCurrentDevice() const override;
    
    void setCallback(AudioCallback callback) override;
    
    bool setLoopback(bool enabled);
    bool isLoopbackEnabled() const { return m_loopback; }
    
private:
    void captureThread();
    bool initializeAudioClient();
    void cleanupAudioClient();
    std::string getDeviceFriendlyName(IMMDevice* device);
    
    // COM interfaces
    IMMDeviceEnumerator* m_deviceEnumerator{nullptr};
    IMMDevice* m_device{nullptr};
    IAudioClient* m_audioClient{nullptr};
    IAudioCaptureClient* m_captureClient{nullptr};
    
    // Render client for loopback
    IAudioRenderClient* m_renderClient{nullptr};
    
    WAVEFORMATEX* m_waveFormat{nullptr};
    HANDLE m_audioEvent{nullptr};
    
    std::unique_ptr<std::thread> m_captureThread;
    std::atomic<bool> m_running{false};
    std::atomic<bool> m_shouldStop{false};
    
    AudioCallback m_callback;
    std::mutex m_callbackMutex;
    
    int m_sampleRate{48000};
    int m_bufferSize{512};
    int m_channels{2};
    bool m_loopback{true};  // System audio capture
    
    std::string m_currentDeviceId;
    
    // Buffer for format conversion
    std::vector<float> m_conversionBuffer;
};

} // namespace SoundBoost

#endif // PLATFORM_WINDOWS
```

```cpp
// src/platform/windows/WASAPICapture.cpp
#ifdef PLATFORM_WINDOWS

#include "WASAPICapture.hpp"
#include "../../utils/Logger.hpp"

#include <comdef.h>
#include <Audioclient.h>
#include <avrt.h>

#pragma comment(lib, "avrt.lib")

namespace SoundBoost {

// Helper for COM initialization
class COMInitializer {
public:
    COMInitializer() {
        HRESULT hr = CoInitializeEx(nullptr, COINIT_MULTITHREADED);
        m_initialized = SUCCEEDED(hr);
    }
    ~COMInitializer() {
        if (m_initialized) CoUninitialize();
    }
    bool isInitialized() const { return m_initialized; }
private:
    bool m_initialized{false};
};

WASAPICapture::WASAPICapture() {
    // Initialize COM
    CoInitializeEx(nullptr, COINIT_MULTITHREADED);
    
    // Create device enumerator
    HRESULT hr = CoCreateInstance(
        __uuidof(MMDeviceEnumerator),
        nullptr,
        CLSCTX_ALL,
        __uuidof(IMMDeviceEnumerator),
        reinterpret_cast<void**>(&m_deviceEnumerator)
    );
    
    if (FAILED(hr)) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to create device enumerator: 0x{:08X}", hr);
    }
}

WASAPICapture::~WASAPICapture() {
    stop();
    cleanupAudioClient();
    
    if (m_deviceEnumerator) {
        m_deviceEnumerator->Release();
    }
    
    CoUninitialize();
}

bool WASAPICapture::initialize(int sampleRate, int bufferSize, int channels) {
    m_sampleRate = sampleRate;
    m_bufferSize = bufferSize;
    m_channels = channels;
    
    // Get default audio endpoint
    HRESULT hr = m_deviceEnumerator->GetDefaultAudioEndpoint(
        m_loopback ? eRender : eCapture,
        eConsole,
        &m_device
    );
    
    if (FAILED(hr)) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to get default audio endpoint: 0x{:08X}", hr);
        return false;
    }
    
    // Get device ID
    LPWSTR deviceId = nullptr;
    m_device->GetId(&deviceId);
    if (deviceId) {
        // Convert to string
        int size = WideCharToMultiByte(CP_UTF8, 0, deviceId, -1, nullptr, 0, nullptr, nullptr);
        m_currentDeviceId.resize(size);
        WideCharToMultiByte(CP_UTF8, 0, deviceId, -1, m_currentDeviceId.data(), size, nullptr, nullptr);
        CoTaskMemFree(deviceId);
    }
    
    return initializeAudioClient();
}

bool WASAPICapture::initializeAudioClient() {
    cleanupAudioClient();
    
    // Activate audio client
    HRESULT hr = m_device->Activate(
        __uuidof(IAudioClient),
        CLSCTX_ALL,
        nullptr,
        reinterpret_cast<void**>(&m_audioClient)
    );
    
    if (FAILED(hr)) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to activate audio client: 0x{:08X}", hr);
        return false;
    }
    
    // Get mix format
    hr = m_audioClient->GetMixFormat(&m_waveFormat);
    if (FAILED(hr)) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to get mix format: 0x{:08X}", hr);
        return false;
    }
    
    LOG_INFO("WASAPI format: {}Hz, {} channels, {} bits",
        m_waveFormat->nSamplesPerSec,
        m_waveFormat->nChannels,
        m_waveFormat->wBitsPerSample);
    
    // Calculate buffer size in 100-nanosecond units
    REFERENCE_TIME bufferDuration = static_cast<REFERENCE_TIME>(
        10000000.0 * m_bufferSize / m_waveFormat->nSamplesPerSec
    );
    
    // Initialize audio client
    DWORD streamFlags = m_loopback ? AUDCLNT_STREAMFLAGS_LOOPBACK : 0;
    streamFlags |= AUDCLNT_STREAMFLAGS_EVENTCALLBACK;
    
    hr = m_audioClient->Initialize(
        AUDCLNT_SHAREMODE_SHARED,
        streamFlags,
        bufferDuration,
        0,
        m_waveFormat,
        nullptr
    );
    
    if (FAILED(hr)) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to initialize audio client: 0x{:08X}", hr);
        return false;
    }
    
    // Create event for buffer notifications
    m_audioEvent = CreateEvent(nullptr, FALSE, FALSE, nullptr);
    if (!m_audioEvent) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to create audio event");
        return false;
    }
    
    hr = m_audioClient->SetEventHandle(m_audioEvent);
    if (FAILED(hr)) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to set event handle: 0x{:08X}", hr);
        return false;
    }
    
    // Get capture client
    hr = m_audioClient->GetService(
        __uuidof(IAudioCaptureClient),
        reinterpret_cast<void**>(&m_captureClient)
    );
    
    if (FAILED(hr)) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to get capture client: 0x{:08X}", hr);
        return false;
    }
    
    // Allocate conversion buffer
    m_conversionBuffer.resize(m_bufferSize * m_waveFormat->nChannels);
    
    LOG_INFO("WASAPI capture initialized successfully");
    return true;
}

void WASAPICapture::cleanupAudioClient() {
    if (m_captureClient) {
        m_captureClient->Release();
        m_captureClient = nullptr;
    }
    
    if (m_audioClient) {
        m_audioClient->Release();
        m_audioClient = nullptr;
    }
    
    if (m_waveFormat) {
        CoTaskMemFree(m_waveFormat);
        m_waveFormat = nullptr;
    }
    
    if (m_audioEvent) {
        CloseHandle(m_audioEvent);
        m_audioEvent = nullptr;
    }
}

void WASAPICapture::start() {
    if (m_running.exchange(true)) {
        return; // Already running
    }
    
    m_shouldStop.store(false);
    
    // Start audio client
    HRESULT hr = m_audioClient->Start();
    if (FAILED(hr)) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to start audio client: 0x{:08X}", hr);
        m_running.store(false);
        return;
    }
    
    // Start capture thread
    m_captureThread = std::make_unique<std::thread>([this]() {
        captureThread();
    });
    
    LOG_INFO("WASAPI capture started");
}

void WASAPICapture::stop() {
    if (!m_running.exchange(false)) {
        return; // Already stopped
    }
    
    m_shouldStop.store(true);
    
    // Signal event to wake up capture thread
    if (m_audioEvent) {
        SetEvent(m_audioEvent);
    }
    
    // Wait for capture thread
    if (m_captureThread && m_captureThread->joinable()) {
        m_captureThread->join();
    }
    
    // Stop audio client
    if (m_audioClient) {
        m_audioClient->Stop();
    }
    
    LOG_INFO("WASAPI capture stopped");
}

void WASAPICapture::captureThread() {
    // Set thread to high priority for audio
    DWORD taskIndex = 0;
    HANDLE avrtHandle = AvSetMmThreadCharacteristicsW(L"Pro Audio", &taskIndex);
    
    if (avrtHandle) {
        AvSetMmThreadPriority(avrtHandle, AVRT_PRIORITY_CRITICAL);
    }
    
    while (!m_shouldStop.load()) {
        // Wait for buffer event
        DWORD waitResult = WaitForSingleObject(m_audioEvent, 100);
        
        if (waitResult != WAIT_OBJECT_0) {
            continue;
        }
        
        if (m_shouldStop.load()) {
            break;
        }
        
        UINT32 packetLength = 0;
        HRESULT hr = m_captureClient->GetNextPacketSize(&packetLength);
        
        if (FAILED(hr)) {
            continue;
        }
        
        while (packetLength > 0 && !m_shouldStop.load()) {
            BYTE* data;
            UINT32 numFrames;
            DWORD flags;
            
            hr = m_captureClient->GetBuffer(&data, &numFrames, &flags, nullptr, nullptr);
            
            if (FAILED(hr)) {
                break;
            }
            
            if (numFrames > 0) {
                // Convert to float if needed
                AudioBuffer buffer(numFrames, m_waveFormat->nChannels, m_waveFormat->nSamplesPerSec);
                
                if (m_waveFormat->wFormatTag == WAVE_FORMAT_IEEE_FLOAT ||
                    (m_waveFormat->wFormatTag == WAVE_FORMAT_EXTENSIBLE &&
                     reinterpret_cast<WAVEFORMATEXTENSIBLE*>(m_waveFormat)->SubFormat == KSDATAFORMAT_SUBTYPE_IEEE_FLOAT)) {
                    // Already float
                    buffer.setData(reinterpret_cast<float*>(data), numFrames * m_waveFormat->nChannels);
                } else if (m_waveFormat->wBitsPerSample == 16) {
                    // Convert from 16-bit
                    const int16_t* srcData = reinterpret_cast<const int16_t*>(data);
                    float* dstData = buffer.getData();
                    for (UINT32 i = 0; i < numFrames * m_waveFormat->nChannels; ++i) {
                        dstData[i] = srcData[i] / 32768.0f;
                    }
                } else if (m_waveFormat->wBitsPerSample == 24) {
                    // Convert from 24-bit
                    const uint8_t* srcData = data;
                    float* dstData = buffer.getData();
                    for (UINT32 i = 0; i < numFrames * m_waveFormat->nChannels; ++i) {
                        int32_t sample = (srcData[i * 3] << 8) | (srcData[i * 3 + 1] << 16) | (srcData[i * 3 + 2] << 24);
                        dstData[i] = sample / 2147483648.0f;
                    }
                }
                
                // Handle silent buffer
                if (flags & AUDCLNT_BUFFERFLAGS_SILENT) {
                    buffer.clear();
                }
                
                // Call callback
                std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(m_callbackMutex);
                if (m_callback) {
                    m_callback(buffer);
                }
            }
            
            m_captureClient->ReleaseBuffer(numFrames);
            
            hr = m_captureClient->GetNextPacketSize(&packetLength);
            if (FAILED(hr)) {
                break;
            }
        }
    }
    
    if (avrtHandle) {
        AvRevertMmThreadCharacteristics(avrtHandle);
    }
}

std::vector<AudioDevice> WASAPICapture::getAvailableDevices() {
    std::vector<AudioDevice> devices;
    
    if (!m_deviceEnumerator) return devices;
    
    IMMDeviceCollection* deviceCollection = nullptr;
    HRESULT hr = m_deviceEnumerator->EnumAudioEndpoints(
        m_loopback ? eRender : eCapture,
        DEVICE_STATE_ACTIVE,
        &deviceCollection
    );
    
    if (FAILED(hr)) {
        return devices;
    }
    
    UINT count = 0;
    deviceCollection->GetCount(&count);
    
    for (UINT i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
        IMMDevice* device = nullptr;
        if (SUCCEEDED(deviceCollection->Item(i, &device))) {
            AudioDevice audioDevice;
            
            // Get device ID
            LPWSTR deviceId = nullptr;
            if (SUCCEEDED(device->GetId(&deviceId))) {
                int size = WideCharToMultiByte(CP_UTF8, 0, deviceId, -1, nullptr, 0, nullptr, nullptr);
                audioDevice.id.resize(size);
                WideCharToMultiByte(CP_UTF8, 0, deviceId, -1, audioDevice.id.data(), size, nullptr, nullptr);
                CoTaskMemFree(deviceId);
            }
            
            // Get device name
            audioDevice.name = getDeviceFriendlyName(device);
            audioDevice.isDefault = (i == 0);
            audioDevice.isInput = !m_loopback;
            audioDevice.sampleRates = {44100, 48000, 96000};
            
            devices.push_back(audioDevice);
            device->Release();
        }
    }
    
    deviceCollection->Release();
    return devices;
}

std::string WASAPICapture::getDeviceFriendlyName(IMMDevice* device) {
    IPropertyStore* props = nullptr;
    HRESULT hr = device->OpenPropertyStore(STGM_READ, &props);
    
    if (FAILED(hr)) return "Unknown Device";
    
    PROPVARIANT varName;
    PropVariantInit(&varName);
    
    hr = props->GetValue(PKEY_Device_FriendlyName, &varName);
    
    std::string name = "Unknown Device";
    if (SUCCEEDED(hr) && varName.vt == VT_LPWSTR) {
        int size = WideCharToMultiByte(CP_UTF8, 0, varName.pwszVal, -1, nullptr, 0, nullptr, nullptr);
        name.resize(size);
        WideCharToMultiByte(CP_UTF8, 0, varName.pwszVal, -1, name.data(), size, nullptr, nullptr);
    }
    
    PropVariantClear(&varName);
    props->Release();
    
    return name;
}

bool WASAPICapture::setDevice(const std::string& deviceId) {
    bool wasRunning = m_running.load();
    if (wasRunning) stop();
    
    if (m_device) {
        m_device->Release();
        m_device = nullptr;
    }
    
    // Convert device ID to wide string
    int wideSize = MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, 0, deviceId.c_str(), -1, nullptr, 0);
    std::wstring wideId(wideSize, 0);
    MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, 0, deviceId.c_str(), -1, wideId.data(), wideSize);
    
    HRESULT hr = m_deviceEnumerator->GetDevice(wideId.c_str(), &m_device);
    
    if (FAILED(hr)) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to get device: 0x{:08X}", hr);
        return false;
    }
    
    m_currentDeviceId = deviceId;
    
    if (!initializeAudioClient()) {
        return false;
    }
    
    if (wasRunning) start();
    
    return true;
}

std::string WASAPICapture::getCurrentDevice() const {
    return m_currentDeviceId;
}

void WASAPICapture::setCallback(AudioCallback callback) {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(m_callbackMutex);
    m_callback = std::move(callback);
}

bool WASAPICapture::setLoopback(bool enabled) {
    m_loopback = enabled;
    return true;
}

} // namespace SoundBoost

#endif // PLATFORM_WINDOWS
```

## Linux PulseAudio Capture

```cpp
// src/platform/linux/PulseAudioCapture.hpp
#pragma once

#ifdef PLATFORM_LINUX

#include "../AudioCaptureBase.hpp"
#include <pulse/pulseaudio.h>

#include <thread>
#include <atomic>
#include <mutex>
#include <condition_variable>

namespace SoundBoost {

class PulseAudioCapture : public AudioCaptureBase {
public:
    PulseAudioCapture();
    ~PulseAudioCapture() override;
    
    bool initialize(int sampleRate, int bufferSize, int channels) override;
    void start() override;
    void stop() override;
    bool isRunning() const override { return m_running.load(); }
    
    std::vector<AudioDevice> getAvailableDevices() override;
    bool setDevice(const std::string& deviceId) override;
    std::string getCurrentDevice() const override;
    
    void setCallback(AudioCallback callback) override;
    
    bool setMonitorMode(bool enabled);
    
private:
    void mainLoop();
    
    static void contextStateCallback(pa_context* c, void* userdata);
    static void streamReadCallback(pa_stream* s, size_t length, void* userdata);
    static void streamStateCallback(pa_stream* s, void* userdata);
    static void sinkInfoCallback(pa_context* c, const pa_sink_info* i, int eol, void* userdata);
    static void sourceInfoCallback(pa_context* c, const pa_source_info* i, int eol, void* userdata);
    
    pa_threaded_mainloop* m_mainloop{nullptr};
    pa_context* m_context{nullptr};
    pa_stream* m_stream{nullptr};
    
    std::atomic<bool> m_running{false};
    std::atomic<bool> m_contextReady{false};
    
    AudioCallback m_callback;
    std::mutex m_callbackMutex;
    
    int m_sampleRate{48000};
    int m_bufferSize{512};
    int m_channels{2};
    bool m_monitorMode{true};  // Monitor system audio
    
    std::string m_currentDeviceId;
    
    // Device enumeration
    std::vector<AudioDevice> m_devices;
    std::mutex m_devicesMutex;
    std::condition_variable m_devicesCv;
    bool m_devicesReady{false};
};

} // namespace SoundBoost

#endif // PLATFORM_LINUX
```

```cpp
// src/platform/linux/PulseAudioCapture.cpp
#ifdef PLATFORM_LINUX

#include "PulseAudioCapture.hpp"
#include "../../utils/Logger.hpp"

namespace SoundBoost {

PulseAudioCapture::PulseAudioCapture() = default;

PulseAudioCapture::~PulseAudioCapture() {
    stop();
    
    if (m_stream) {
        pa_stream_unref(m_stream);
    }
    
    if (m_context) {
        pa_context_disconnect(m_context);
        pa_context_unref(m_context);
    }
    
    if (m_mainloop) {
        pa_threaded_mainloop_stop(m_mainloop);
        pa_threaded_mainloop_free(m_mainloop);
    }
}

bool PulseAudioCapture::initialize(int sampleRate, int bufferSize, int channels) {
    m_sampleRate = sampleRate;
    m_bufferSize = bufferSize;
    m_channels = channels;
    
    // Create mainloop
    m_mainloop = pa_threaded_mainloop_new();
    if (!m_mainloop) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to create PulseAudio mainloop");
        return false;
    }
    
    // Get mainloop API
    pa_mainloop_api* api = pa_threaded_mainloop_get_api(m_mainloop);
    
    // Create context
    m_context = pa_context_new(api, "SoundBoost Pro");
    if (!m_context) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to create PulseAudio context");
        return false;
    }
    
    // Set context state callback
    pa_context_set_state_callback(m_context, contextStateCallback, this);
    
    // Connect to server
    if (pa_context_connect(m_context, nullptr, PA_CONTEXT_NOFLAGS, nullptr) < 0) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to connect to PulseAudio server");
        return false;
    }
    
    // Start mainloop
    if (pa_threaded_mainloop_start(m_mainloop) < 0) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to start PulseAudio mainloop");
        return false;
    }
    
    // Wait for context to be ready
    pa_threaded_mainloop_lock(m_mainloop);
    while (!m_contextReady.load()) {
        pa_threaded_mainloop_wait(m_mainloop);
    }
    
    pa_context_state_t state = pa_context_get_state(m_context);
    if (state != PA_CONTEXT_READY) {
        pa_threaded_mainloop_unlock(m_mainloop);
        LOG_ERROR("PulseAudio context failed to become ready");
        return false;
    }
    pa_threaded_mainloop_unlock(m_mainloop);
    
    // Create stream
    pa_sample_spec spec;
    spec.format = PA_SAMPLE_FLOAT32LE;
    spec.rate = sampleRate;
    spec.channels = channels;
    
    pa_threaded_mainloop_lock(m_mainloop);
    
    m_stream = pa_stream_new(m_context, "SoundBoost Capture", &spec, nullptr);
    if (!m_stream) {
        pa_threaded_mainloop_unlock(m_mainloop);
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to create PulseAudio stream");
        return false;
    }
    
    pa_stream_set_state_callback(m_stream, streamStateCallback, this);
    pa_stream_set_read_callback(m_stream, streamReadCallback, this);
    
    pa_threaded_mainloop_unlock(m_mainloop);
    
    LOG_INFO("PulseAudio capture initialized: {}Hz, {} channels", sampleRate, channels);
    return true;
}

void PulseAudioCapture::contextStateCallback(pa_context* c, void* userdata) {
    auto* capture = static_cast<PulseAudioCapture*>(userdata);
    
    pa_context_state_t state = pa_context_get_state(c);
    
    switch (state) {
        case PA_CONTEXT_READY:
        case PA_CONTEXT_FAILED:
        case PA_CONTEXT_TERMINATED:
            capture->m_contextReady.store(true);
            pa_threaded_mainloop_signal(capture->m_mainloop, 0);
            break;
        default:
            break;
    }
}

void PulseAudioCapture::streamStateCallback(pa_stream* s, void* userdata) {
    auto* capture = static_cast<PulseAudioCapture*>(userdata);
    pa_threaded_mainloop_signal(capture->m_mainloop, 0);
}

void PulseAudioCapture::streamReadCallback(pa_stream* s, size_t length, void* userdata) {
    auto* capture = static_cast<PulseAudioCapture*>(userdata);
    
    const void* data;
    size_t nbytes;
    
    if (pa_stream_peek(s, &data, &nbytes) < 0) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to read from PulseAudio stream");
        return;
    }
    
    if (data && nbytes > 0) {
        // Create audio buffer
        size_t numSamples = nbytes / sizeof(float) / capture->m_channels;
        AudioBuffer buffer(numSamples, capture->m_channels, capture->m_sampleRate);
        buffer.setData(static_cast<const float*>(data), nbytes / sizeof(float));
        
        // Call callback
        std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(capture->m_callbackMutex);
        if (capture->m_callback) {
            capture->m_callback(buffer);
        }
    }
    
    pa_stream_drop(s);
}

void PulseAudioCapture::start() {
    if (m_running.exchange(true)) {
        return;
    }
    
    pa_threaded_mainloop_lock(m_mainloop);
    
    // Get default monitor source for system audio
    std::string sourceName;
    if (m_monitorMode) {
        // Use default sink's monitor
        sourceName = m_currentDeviceId.empty() ? 
            "@DEFAULT_MONITOR@" : m_currentDeviceId + ".monitor";
    } else {
        sourceName = m_currentDeviceId;
    }
    
    pa_buffer_attr bufferAttr;
    bufferAttr.maxlength = (uint32_t)-1;
    bufferAttr.tlength = (uint32_t)-1;
    bufferAttr.prebuf = (uint32_t)-1;
    bufferAttr.minreq = (uint32_t)-1;
    bufferAttr.fragsize = m_bufferSize * m_channels * sizeof(float);
    
    if (pa_stream_connect_record(m_stream, sourceName.c_str(), &bufferAttr,
            static_cast<pa_stream_flags_t>(PA_STREAM_ADJUST_LATENCY)) < 0) {
        LOG_ERROR("Failed to connect PulseAudio stream");
        m_running.store(false);
        pa_threaded_mainloop_unlock(m_mainloop);
        return;
    }
    
    // Wait for stream to be ready
    while (true) {
        pa_stream_state_t state = pa_stream_get_state(m_stream);
        if (state == PA_STREAM_READY) break;
        if (!PA_STREAM_IS_GOOD(state)) {
            LOG_ERROR("PulseAudio stream failed");
            m_running.store(false);
            pa_threaded_mainloop_unlock(m_mainloop);
            return;
        }
        pa_threaded_mainloop_wait(m_mainloop);
    }
    
    pa_threaded_mainloop_unlock(m_mainloop);
    
    LOG_INFO("PulseAudio capture started");
}

void PulseAudioCapture::stop() {
    if (!m_running.exchange(false)) {
        return;
    }
    
    pa_threaded_mainloop_lock(m_mainloop);
    
    if (m_stream) {
        pa_stream_disconnect(m_stream);
    }
    
    pa_threaded_mainloop_unlock(m_mainloop);
    
    LOG_INFO("PulseAudio capture stopped");
}

void PulseAudioCapture::sinkInfoCallback(pa_context* c, const pa_sink_info* i, int eol, void* userdata) {
    auto* capture = static_cast<PulseAudioCapture*>(userdata);
    
    if (eol > 0) {
        capture->m_devicesReady = true;
        capture->m_devicesCv.notify_all();
        pa_threaded_mainloop_signal(capture->m_mainloop, 0);
        return;
    }
    
    if (i) {
        AudioDevice device;
        device.id = i->name;
        device.name = i->description ? i->description : i->name;
        device.isInput = false;
        device.isDefault = (i->flags & PA_SINK_DEFAULT);
        device.sampleRates = {44100, 48000, 96000};
        
        std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(capture->m_devicesMutex);
        capture->m_devices.push_back(device);
    }
}

std::vector<AudioDevice> PulseAudioCapture::getAvailableDevices() {
    m_devices.clear();
    m_devicesReady = false;
    
    pa_threaded_mainloop_lock(m_mainloop);
    
    pa_operation* op = pa_context_get_sink_info_list(m_context, sinkInfoCallback, this);
    
    while (!m_devicesReady) {
        pa_threaded_mainloop_wait(m_mainloop);
    }
    
    if (op) {
        pa_operation_unref(op);
    }
    
    pa_threaded_mainloop_unlock(m_mainloop);
    
    return m_devices;
}

bool PulseAudioCapture::setDevice(const std::string& deviceId) {
    bool wasRunning = m_running.load();
    if (wasRunning) stop();
    
    m_currentDeviceId = deviceId;
    
    if (wasRunning) start();
    
    return true;
}

std::string PulseAudioCapture::getCurrentDevice() const {
    return m_currentDeviceId;
}

void PulseAudioCapture::setCallback(AudioCallback callback) {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(m_callbackMutex);
    m_callback = std::move(callback);
}

bool PulseAudioCapture::setMonitorMode(bool enabled) {
    m_monitorMode = enabled;
    return true;
}

} // namespace SoundBoost

#endif // PLATFORM_LINUX
```

## GUI Components - Spectrum Widget

```cpp
// src/gui/components/SpectrumWidget.hpp
#pragma once

#include <QWidget>
#include <QTimer>
#include <vector>
#include <mutex>

namespace SoundBoost {

class SpectrumWidget : public QWidget {
    Q_OBJECT
    
    Q_PROPERTY(QColor barColor READ barColor WRITE setBarColor)
    Q_PROPERTY(QColor peakColor READ peakColor WRITE setPeakColor)
    Q_PROPERTY(QColor backgroundColor READ backgroundColor WRITE setBackgroundColor)
    Q_PROPERTY(int barCount READ barCount WRITE setBarCount)
    Q_PROPERTY(float peakDecay READ peakDecay WRITE setPeakDecay)
    
public:
    explicit SpectrumWidget(QWidget* parent = nullptr);
    ~SpectrumWidget() override;
    
    void updateData(const std::vector<float>& magnitudes);
    void reset();
    
    // Properties
    QColor barColor() const { return m_barColor; }
    void setBarColor(const QColor& color);
    
    QColor peakColor() const { return m_peakColor; }
    void setPeakColor(const QColor& color);
    
    QColor backgroundColor() const { return m_backgroundColor; }
    void setBackgroundColor(const QColor& color);
    
    int barCount() const { return m_barCount; }
    void setBarCount(int count);
    
    float peakDecay() const { return m_peakDecay; }
    void setPeakDecay(float decay);
    
    // Display modes
    enum class Mode {
        Bars,
        Lines,
        Filled,
        Gradient
    };
    
    void setMode(Mode mode);
    Mode mode() const { return m_mode; }
    
    void setLogScale(bool enabled);
    bool isLogScale() const { return m_logScale; }
    
protected:
    void paintEvent(QPaintEvent* event) override;
    void resizeEvent(QResizeEvent* event) override;
    
private:
    void processData();
    void updatePeaks();
    float mapFrequencyToBar(int freqBin, int numBins, int numBars);
    
    std::vector<float> m_rawMagnitudes;
    std::vector<float> m_smoothedBars;
    std::vector<float> m_peaks;
    std::vector<float> m_peakHoldTimes;
    
    QColor m_barColor{0, 200, 255};
    QColor m_peakColor{255, 100, 100};
    QColor m_backgroundColor{20, 20, 30};
    QColor m_gridColor{50, 50, 60};
    
    int m_barCount{64};
    float m_peakDecay{0.95f};
    float m_smoothingFactor{0.3f};
    float m_peakHoldTime{1.0f};  // seconds
    
    Mode m_mode{Mode::Bars};
    bool m_logScale{true};
    bool m_showPeaks{true};
    bool m_showGrid{true};
    
    QTimer* m_updateTimer;
    std::mutex m_dataMutex;
    
    // Precomputed bar positions
    std::vector<QRectF> m_barRects;
    
    // Gradient for gradient mode
    QLinearGradient m_gradient;
};

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

```cpp
// src/gui/components/SpectrumWidget.cpp
#include "SpectrumWidget.hpp"

#include <QPainter>
#include <QPainterPath>
#include <QLinearGradient>
#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

namespace SoundBoost {

SpectrumWidget::SpectrumWidget(QWidget* parent)
    : QWidget(parent)
    , m_updateTimer(new QTimer(this))
{
    setMinimumSize(200, 100);
    setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy::Expanding, QSizePolicy::Expanding);
    
    m_smoothedBars.resize(m_barCount, 0.0f);
    m_peaks.resize(m_barCount, 0.0f);
    m_peakHoldTimes.resize(m_barCount, 0.0f);
    
    // Setup gradient
    m_gradient.setColorAt(0.0, QColor(0, 200, 255));
    m_gradient.setColorAt(0.5, QColor(0, 255, 100));
    m_gradient.setColorAt(0.8, QColor(255, 255, 0));
    m_gradient.setColorAt(1.0, QColor(255, 50, 50));
    
    // Update timer for smooth animation
    connect(m_updateTimer, &QTimer::timeout, this, [this]() {
        updatePeaks();
        update();
    });
    m_updateTimer->start(16); // ~60 FPS
}

SpectrumWidget::~SpectrumWidget() = default;

void SpectrumWidget::updateData(const std::vector<float>& magnitudes) {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(m_dataMutex);
    m_rawMagnitudes = magnitudes;
    processData();
}

void SpectrumWidget::processData() {
    if (m_rawMagnitudes.empty()) return;
    
    int numBins = m_rawMagnitudes.size();
    
    for (int bar = 0; bar < m_barCount; ++bar) {
        // Map bar to frequency bins
        float startBin, endBin;
        
        if (m_logScale) {
            // Logarithmic frequency mapping
            float logMin = std::log10(20.0f);    // 20 Hz
            float logMax = std::log10(20000.0f); // 20 kHz
            float logRange = logMax - logMin;
            
            float logStart = logMin + (bar / static_cast<float>(m_barCount)) * logRange;
            float logEnd = logMin + ((bar + 1) / static_cast<float>(m_barCount)) * logRange;
            
            float freqStart = std::pow(10.0f, logStart);
            float freqEnd = std::pow(10.0f, logEnd);
            
            // Convert frequency to bin (assuming 48kHz sample rate)
            startBin = freqStart * numBins * 2 / 48000.0f;
            endBin = freqEnd * numBins * 2 / 48000.0f;
        } else {
            // Linear mapping
            startBin = bar * numBins / static_cast<float>(m_barCount);
            endBin = (bar + 1) * numBins / static_cast<float>(m_barCount);
        }
        
        // Clamp to valid range
        int binStart = std::clamp(static_cast<int>(startBin), 0, numBins - 1);
        int binEnd = std::clamp(static_cast<int>(endBin), binStart + 1, numBins);
        
        // Calculate average magnitude for this bar
        float sum = 0.0f;
        for (int bin = binStart; bin < binEnd; ++bin) {
            sum += m_rawMagnitudes[bin];
        }
        float avg = sum / (binEnd - binStart);
        
        // Convert to dB and normalize
        float db = 20.0f * std::log10(std::max(avg, 1e-10f));
        float normalized = (db + 60.0f) / 60.0f; // -60dB to 0dB range
        normalized = std::clamp(normalized, 0.0f, 1.0f);
        
        // Smooth
        m_smoothedBars[bar] = m_smoothedBars[bar] * (1.0f - m_smoothingFactor) + 
                              normalized * m_smoothingFactor;
        
        // Update peaks
        if (m_smoothedBars[bar] >= m_peaks[bar]) {
            m_peaks[bar] = m_smoothedBars[bar];
            m_peakHoldTimes[bar] = m_peakHoldTime;
        }
    }
}

void SpectrumWidget::updatePeaks() {
    float dt = 0.016f; // ~60 FPS
    
    for (int i = 0; i < m_barCount; ++i) {
        if (m_peakHoldTimes[i] > 0) {
            m_peakHoldTimes[i] -= dt;
        } else {
            m_peaks[i] *= m_peakDecay;
        }
    }
}

void SpectrumWidget::paintEvent(QPaintEvent* event) {
    Q_UNUSED(event);
    
    QPainter painter(this);
    painter.setRenderHint(QPainter::Antialiasing);
    
    // Background
    painter.fillRect(rect(), m_backgroundColor);
    
    // Draw grid
    if (m_showGrid) {
        painter.setPen(QPen(m_gridColor, 1));
        
        // Horizontal grid lines (dB levels)
        for (int i = 1; i < 6; ++i) {
            int y = height() * i / 6;
            painter.drawLine(0, y, width(), y);
        }
        
        // Vertical grid lines (frequency markers)
        if (m_logScale) {
            std::vector<float> freqs = {50, 100, 200, 500, 1000, 2000, 5000, 10000};
            for (float freq : freqs) {
                float logPos = (std::log10(freq) - std::log10(20.0f)) / 
                              (std::log10(20000.0f) - std::log10(20.0f));
                int x = static_cast<int>(logPos * width());
                painter.drawLine(x, 0, x, height());
            }
        }
    }
    
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(m_dataMutex);
    
    if (m_smoothedBars.empty()) return;
    
    float barWidth = static_cast<float>(width()) / m_barCount;
    float gap = std::max(1.0f, barWidth * 0.1f);
    float actualBarWidth = barWidth - gap;
    
    switch (m_mode) {
        case Mode::Bars:
            for (int i = 0; i < m_barCount; ++i) {
                float barHeight = m_smoothedBars[i] * height();
                float x = i * barWidth;
                float y = height() - barHeight;
                
                // Draw bar with gradient
                QLinearGradient barGradient(x, height(), x, y);
                barGradient.setColorAt(0.0, m_barColor.darker(150));
                barGradient.setColorAt(1.0, m_barColor);
                
                painter.fillRect(QRectF(x, y, actualBarWidth, barHeight), barGradient);
                
                // Draw peak
                if (m_showPeaks && m_peaks[i] > 0.01f) {
                    float peakY = height() - m_peaks[i] * height();
                    painter.fillRect(QRectF(x, peakY - 2, actualBarWidth, 2), m_peakColor);
                }
            }
            break;
            
        case Mode::Lines: {
            QPainterPath path;
            path.moveTo(0, height());
            
            for (int i = 0; i < m_barCount; ++i) {
                float x = i * barWidth + actualBarWidth / 2;
                float y = height() - m_smoothedBars[i] * height();
                
                if (i == 0) {
                    path.lineTo(x, y);
                } else {
                    // Smooth curve
                    float prevX = (i - 1) * barWidth + actualBarWidth / 2;
                    float prevY = height() - m_smoothedBars[i - 1] * height();
                    float ctrlX = (prevX + x) / 2;
                    path.quadTo(ctrlX, prevY, x, y);
                }
            }
            
            path.lineTo(width(), height());
            path.closeSubpath();
            
            // Fill
            QLinearGradient fillGradient(0, height(), 0, 0);
            fillGradient.setColorAt(0.0, m_barColor.darker(200));
            fillGradient.setColorAt(1.0, m_barColor);
            painter.fillPath(path, fillGradient);
            
            // Stroke
            painter.setPen(QPen(m_barColor.lighter(150), 2));
            painter.drawPath(path);
            break;
        }
            
        case Mode::Gradient: {
            m_gradient.setStart(0, height());
            m_gradient.setFinalStop(0, 0);
            
            for (int i = 0; i < m_barCount; ++i) {
                float barHeight = m_smoothedBars[i] * height();
                float x = i * barWidth;
                float y = height() - barHeight;
                
                painter.fillRect(QRectF(x, y, actualBarWidth, barHeight), m_gradient);
            }
            break;
        }
            
        case Mode::Filled:
        default:
            break;
    }
}

void SpectrumWidget::resizeEvent(QResizeEvent* event) {
    QWidget::resizeEvent(event);
    update();
}

void SpectrumWidget::reset() {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(m_dataMutex);
    
    std::fill(m_smoothedBars.begin(), m_smoothedBars.end(), 0.0f);
    std::fill(m_peaks.begin(), m_peaks.end(), 0.0f);
    std::fill(m_peakHoldTimes.begin(), m_peakHoldTimes.end(), 0.0f);
    
    update();
}

void SpectrumWidget::setBarColor(const QColor& color) {
    m_barColor = color;
    update();
}

void SpectrumWidget::setPeakColor(const QColor& color) {
    m_peakColor = color;
    update();
}

void SpectrumWidget::setBackgroundColor(const QColor& color) {
    m_backgroundColor = color;
    update();
}

void SpectrumWidget::setBarCount(int count) {
    m_barCount = std::clamp(count, 8, 256);
    m_smoothedBars.resize(m_barCount, 0.0f);
    m_peaks.resize(m_barCount, 0.0f);
    m_peakHoldTimes.resize(m_barCount, 0.0f);
    update();
}

void SpectrumWidget::setPeakDecay(float decay) {
    m_peakDecay = std::clamp(decay, 0.8f, 0.999f);
}

void SpectrumWidget::setMode(Mode mode) {
    m_mode = mode;
    update();
}

void SpectrumWidget::setLogScale(bool enabled) {
    m_logScale = enabled;
    update();
}

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

## VU Meter Widget

```cpp
// src/gui/components/VUMeter.hpp
#pragma once

#include <QWidget>
#include <QTimer>

namespace SoundBoost {

class VUMeter : public QWidget {
    Q_OBJECT
    
    Q_PROPERTY(float level READ level WRITE setLevel)
    Q_PROPERTY(float peakLevel READ peakLevel)
    Q_PROPERTY(bool stereo READ isStereo WRITE setStereo)
    
public:
    explicit VUMeter(QWidget* parent = nullptr);
    ~VUMeter() override;
    
    float level() const { return m_leftLevel; }
    void setLevel(float level);
    void setLevels(float left, float right);
    
    float peakLevel() const { return std::max(m_leftPeak, m_rightPeak); }
    
    bool isStereo() const { return m_stereo; }
    void setStereo(bool stereo);
    
    void setOrientation(Qt::Orientation orientation);
    Qt::Orientation orientation() const { return m_orientation; }
    
    void reset();
    
protected:
    void paintEvent(QPaintEvent* event) override;
    
private:
    void updatePeaks();
    QColor levelToColor(float level) const;
    
    float m_leftLevel{0.0f};
    float m_rightLevel{0.0f};
    float m_leftPeak{0.0f};
    float m_rightPeak{0.0f};
    float m_leftPeakHold{0.0f};
    float m_rightPeakHold{0.0f};
    
    float m_peakDecay{0.95f};
    float m_peakHoldTime{1.5f};
    float m_peakHoldCounter{0.0f};
    
    bool m_stereo{true};
    Qt::Orientation m_orientation{Qt::Vertical};
    
    QTimer* m_updateTimer;
    
    // Colors
    QColor m_greenColor{0, 200, 0};
    QColor m_yellowColor{255, 200, 0};
    QColor m_redColor{255, 50, 50};
    QColor m_backgroundColor{30, 30, 40};
    QColor m_peakColor{255, 255, 255};
    
    // Thresholds (in linear, not dB)
    float m_yellowThreshold{0.7f};
    float m_redThreshold{0.9f};
};

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

```cpp
// src/gui/components/VUMeter.cpp
#include "VUMeter.hpp"

#include <QPainter>
#include <QLinearGradient>
#include <cmath>

namespace SoundBoost {

VUMeter::VUMeter(QWidget* parent)
    : QWidget(parent)
    , m_updateTimer(new QTimer(this))
{
    setMinimumSize(20, 100);
    
    connect(m_updateTimer, &QTimer::timeout, this, [this]() {
        updatePeaks();
        update();
    });
    m_updateTimer->start(30);
}

VUMeter::~VUMeter() = default;

void VUMeter::setLevel(float level) {
    m_leftLevel = std::clamp(level, 0.0f, 1.0f);
    m_rightLevel = m_leftLevel;
}

void VUMeter::setLevels(float left, float right) {
    m_leftLevel = std::clamp(left, 0.0f, 1.0f);
    m_rightLevel = std::clamp(right, 0.0f, 1.0f);
    
    // Update peaks
    if (m_leftLevel > m_leftPeak) {
        m_leftPeak = m_leftLevel;
        m_leftPeakHold = m_peakHoldTime;
    }
    if (m_rightLevel > m_rightPeak) {
        m_rightPeak = m_rightLevel;
        m_rightPeakHold = m_peakHoldTime;
    }
}

void VUMeter::setStereo(bool stereo) {
    m_stereo = stereo;
    update();
}

void VUMeter::setOrientation(Qt::Orientation orientation) {
    m_orientation = orientation;
    update();
}

void VUMeter::updatePeaks() {
    float dt = 0.03f;
    
    // Left peak
    if (m_leftPeakHold > 0) {
        m_leftPeakHold -= dt;
    } else {
        m_leftPeak *= m_peakDecay;
    }
    
    // Right peak
    if (m_rightPeakHold > 0) {
        m_rightPeakHold -= dt;
    } else {
        m_rightPeak *= m_peakDecay;
    }
}

QColor VUMeter::levelToColor(float level) const {
    if (level >= m_redThreshold) {
        return m_redColor;
    } else if (level >= m_yellowThreshold) {
        float t = (level - m_yellowThreshold) / (m_redThreshold - m_yellowThreshold);
        return QColor(
            m_yellowColor.red() + t * (m_redColor.red() - m_yellowColor.red()),
            m_yellowColor.green() + t * (m_redColor.green() - m_yellowColor.green()),
            m_yellowColor.blue() + t * (m_redColor.blue() - m_yellowColor.blue())
        );
    } else {
        float t = level / m_yellowThreshold;
        return QColor(
            m_greenColor.red() + t * (m_yellowColor.red() - m_greenColor.red()),
            m_greenColor.green() + t * (m_yellowColor.green() - m_greenColor.green()),
            m_greenColor.blue() + t * (m_yellowColor.blue() - m_greenColor.blue())
        );
    }
}

void VUMeter::paintEvent(QPaintEvent* event) {
    Q_UNUSED(event);
    
    QPainter painter(this);
    painter.setRenderHint(QPainter::Antialiasing);
    
    painter.fillRect(rect(), m_backgroundColor);
    
    int padding = 2;
    int gap = m_stereo ? 4 : 0;
    
    if (m_orientation == Qt::Vertical) {
        int meterWidth = (width() - 2 * padding - gap) / (m_stereo ? 2 : 1);
        int meterHeight = height() - 2 * padding;
        
        // Left meter
        QRect leftRect(padding, padding, meterWidth, meterHeight);
        drawMeter(painter, leftRect, m_leftLevel, m_leftPeak);
        
        // Right meter
        if (m_stereo) {
            QRect rightRect(padding + meterWidth + gap, padding, meterWidth, meterHeight);
            drawMeter(painter, rightRect, m_rightLevel, m_rightPeak);
        }
    } else {
        int meterHeight = (height() - 2 * padding - gap) / (m_stereo ? 2 : 1);
        int meterWidth = width() - 2 * padding;
        
        // Left/top meter
        QRect leftRect(padding, padding, meterWidth, meterHeight);
        drawMeterHorizontal(painter, leftRect, m_leftLevel, m_leftPeak);
        
        // Right/bottom meter
        if (m_stereo) {
            QRect rightRect(padding, padding + meterHeight + gap, meterWidth, meterHeight);
            drawMeterHorizontal(painter, rightRect, m_rightLevel, m_rightPeak);
        }
    }
    
    // Scale markers
    painter.setPen(QPen(QColor(100, 100, 100), 1));
    
    // dB scale
    std::vector<float> dbMarks = {0, -3, -6, -12, -20, -40, -60};
    for (float db : dbMarks) {
        float linear = std::pow(10.0f, db / 20.0f);
        
        if (m_orientation == Qt::Vertical) {
            int y = padding + static_cast<int>((1.0f - linear) * (height() - 2 * padding));
            painter.drawLine(0, y, padding, y);
            painter.drawLine(width() - padding, y, width(), y);
        }
    }
}

void VUMeter::drawMeter(QPainter& painter, const QRect& rect, float level, float peak) {
    // Gradient fill
    QLinearGradient gradient(rect.left(), rect.bottom(), rect.left(), rect.top());
    gradient.setColorAt(0.0, m_greenColor);
    gradient.setColorAt(m_yellowThreshold, m_yellowColor);
    gradient.setColorAt(m_redThreshold, m_redColor);
    gradient.setColorAt(1.0, m_redColor);
    
    // Calculate filled height
    int fillHeight = static_cast<int>(level * rect.height());
    QRect fillRect(rect.left(), rect.bottom() - fillHeight, rect.width(), fillHeight);
    
    // Draw background (unfilled part)
    painter.fillRect(rect, m_backgroundColor.darker(120));
    
    // Draw filled part
    painter.fillRect(fillRect, gradient);
    
    // Draw segments
    painter.setPen(QPen(m_backgroundColor, 1));
    int segmentHeight = rect.height() / 30;
    for (int y = rect.top(); y < rect.bottom(); y += segmentHeight) {
        painter.drawLine(rect.left(), y, rect.right(), y);
    }
    
    // Draw peak indicator
    if (peak > 0.01f) {
        int peakY = rect.bottom() - static_cast<int>(peak * rect.height());
        painter.fillRect(rect.left(), peakY - 1, rect.width(), 2, m_peakColor);
    }
    
    // Clip indicator
    if (level >= 1.0f) {
        painter.fillRect(rect.left(), rect.top(), rect.width(), 4, m_redColor);
    }
}

void VUMeter::drawMeterHorizontal(QPainter& painter, const QRect& rect, float level, float peak) {
    // Similar to vertical but horizontal
    QLinearGradient gradient(rect.left(), rect.top(), rect.right(), rect.top());
    gradient.setColorAt(0.0, m_greenColor);
    gradient.setColorAt(m_yellowThreshold, m_yellowColor);
    gradient.setColorAt(m_redThreshold, m_redColor);
    
    int fillWidth = static_cast<int>(level * rect.width());
    QRect fillRect(rect.left(), rect.top(), fillWidth, rect.height());
    
    painter.fillRect(rect, m_backgroundColor.darker(120));
    painter.fillRect(fillRect, gradient);
    
    // Peak indicator
    if (peak > 0.01f) {
        int peakX = rect.left() + static_cast<int>(peak * rect.width());
        painter.fillRect(peakX - 1, rect.top(), 2, rect.height(), m_peakColor);
    }
}

void VUMeter::reset() {
    m_leftLevel = 0.0f;
    m_rightLevel = 0.0f;
    m_leftPeak = 0.0f;
    m_rightPeak = 0.0f;
    update();
}

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

## Logger Implementation

```cpp
// src/utils/Logger.hpp
#pragma once

#include <string>
#include <memory>
#include <mutex>
#include <fstream>
#include <sstream>
#include <chrono>
#include <source_location>

namespace SoundBoost {

enum class LogLevel {
    Trace = 0,
    Debug = 1,
    Info = 2,
    Warning = 3,
    Error = 4,
    Critical = 5,
    Off = 6
};

class Logger {
public:
    static Logger& getInstance();
    
    void initialize(LogLevel level = LogLevel::Info, 
                   const std::string& logFile = "");
    void shutdown();
    
    void setLevel(LogLevel level) { m_level = level; }
    LogLevel getLevel() const { return m_level; }
    
    void setConsoleOutput(bool enabled) { m_consoleOutput = enabled; }
    void setFileOutput(bool enabled, const std::string& path = "");
    
    template<typename... Args>
    void log(LogLevel level, const std::source_location& loc, 
             std::string_view format, Args&&... args) {
        if (level < m_level) return;
        
        std::string message = formatMessage(format, std::forward<Args>(args)...);
        writeLog(level, loc, message);
    }
    
    template<typename... Args>
    void trace(std::string_view format, Args&&... args) {
        log(LogLevel::Trace, std::source_location::current(), format, std::forward<Args>(args)...);
    }
    
    template<typename... Args>
    void debug(std::string_view format, Args&&... args) {
        log(LogLevel::Debug, std::source_location::current(), format, std::forward<Args>(args)...);
    }
    
    template<typename... Args>
    void info(std::string_view format, Args&&... args) {
        log(LogLevel::Info, std::source_location::current(), format, std::forward<Args>(args)...);
    }
    
    template<typename... Args>
    void warning(std::string_view format, Args&&... args) {
        log(LogLevel::Warning, std::source_location::current(), format, std::forward<Args>(args)...);
    }
    
    template<typename... Args>
    void error(std::string_view format, Args&&... args) {
        log(LogLevel::Error, std::source_location::current(), format, std::forward<Args>(args)...);
    }
    
    template<typename... Args>
    void critical(std::string_view format, Args&&... args) {
        log(LogLevel::Critical, std::source_location::current(), format, std::forward<Args>(args)...);
    }
    
private:
    Logger() = default;
    ~Logger();
    
    Logger(const Logger&) = delete;
    Logger& operator=(const Logger&) = delete;
    
    template<typename... Args>
    std::string formatMessage(std::string_view format, Args&&... args);
    
    void writeLog(LogLevel level, const std::source_location& loc, 
                  const std::string& message);
    std::string getTimestamp();
    std::string levelToString(LogLevel level);
    std::string levelToColor(LogLevel level);
    
    LogLevel m_level{LogLevel::Info};
    bool m_consoleOutput{true};
    bool m_fileOutput{false};
    
    std::ofstream m_fileStream;
    std::mutex m_mutex;
    
    bool m_initialized{false};
};

// Convenience macros
#define LOG_TRACE(...) SoundBoost::Logger::getInstance().trace(__VA_ARGS__)
#define LOG_DEBUG(...) SoundBoost::Logger::getInstance().debug(__VA_ARGS__)
#define LOG_INFO(...) SoundBoost::Logger::getInstance().info(__VA_ARGS__)
#define LOG_WARN(...) SoundBoost::Logger::getInstance().warning(__VA_ARGS__)
#define LOG_ERROR(...) SoundBoost::Logger::getInstance().error(__VA_ARGS__)
#define LOG_CRITICAL(...) SoundBoost::Logger::getInstance().critical(__VA_ARGS__)

} // namespace SoundBoost
```

```cpp
// src/utils/Logger.cpp
#include "Logger.hpp"

#include <iostream>
#include <iomanip>
#include <ctime>
#include <filesystem>
#include <format>

namespace SoundBoost {

Logger& Logger::getInstance() {
    static Logger instance;
    return instance;
}

Logger::~Logger() {
    shutdown();
}

void Logger::initialize(LogLevel level, const std::string& logFile) {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(m_mutex);
    
    m_level = level;
    
    if (!logFile.empty()) {
        setFileOutput(true, logFile);
    }
    
    m_initialized = true;
    
    info("Logger initialized at level {}", levelToString(level));
}

void Logger::shutdown() {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(m_mutex);
    
    if (m_fileStream.is_open()) {
        m_fileStream.close();
    }
    
    m_initialized = false;
}

void Logger::setFileOutput(bool enabled, const std::string& path) {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(m_mutex);
    
    if (m_fileStream.is_open()) {
        m_fileStream.close();
    }
    
    m_fileOutput = enabled;
    
    if (enabled && !path.empty()) {
        // Create directory if needed
        std::filesystem::path filePath(path);
        if (filePath.has_parent_path()) {
            std::filesystem::create_directories(filePath.parent_path());
        }
        
        m_fileStream.open(path, std::ios::out | std::ios::app);
        if (!m_fileStream.is_open()) {
            std::cerr << "Failed to open log file: " << path << std::endl;
            m_fileOutput = false;
        }
    }
}

template<typename... Args>
std::string Logger::formatMessage(std::string_view format, Args&&... args) {
    try {
        return std::vformat(format, std::make_format_args(args...));
    } catch (const std::format_error& e) {
        return std::string(format) + " [FORMAT ERROR: " + e.what() + "]";
    }
}

void Logger::writeLog(LogLevel level, const std::source_location& loc, 
                      const std::string& message) {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(m_mutex);
    
    std::string timestamp = getTimestamp();
    std::string levelStr = levelToString(level);
    
    // Extract filename from path
    std::string_view filename = loc.file_name();
    auto lastSlash = filename.find_last_of("/\\");
    if (lastSlash != std::string_view::npos) {
        filename = filename.substr(lastSlash + 1);
    }
    
    std::ostringstream formatted;
    formatted << "[" << timestamp << "] "
              << "[" << levelStr << "] "
              << "[" << filename << ":" << loc.line() << "] "
              << message;
    
    std::string logLine = formatted.str();
    
    // Console output
    if (m_consoleOutput) {
        std::string color = levelToColor(level);
        std::cout << color << logLine << "\033[0m" << std::endl;
    }
    
    // File output
    if (m_fileOutput && m_fileStream.is_open()) {
        m_fileStream << logLine << std::endl;
        m_fileStream.flush();
    }
}

std::string Logger::getTimestamp() {
    auto now = std::chrono::system_clock::now();
    auto time = std::chrono::system_clock::to_time_t(now);
    auto ms = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::milliseconds>(
        now.time_since_epoch()) % 1000;
    
    std::tm tm;
#ifdef _WIN32
    localtime_s(&tm, &time);
#else
    localtime_r(&time, &tm);
#endif
    
    std::ostringstream oss;
    oss << std::put_time(&tm, "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
        << "." << std::setfill('0') << std::setw(3) << ms.count();
    
    return oss.str();
}

std::string Logger::levelToString(LogLevel level) {
    switch (level) {
        case LogLevel::Trace:    return "TRACE";
        case LogLevel::Debug:    return "DEBUG";
        case LogLevel::Info:     return "INFO ";
        case LogLevel::Warning:  return "WARN ";
        case LogLevel::Error:    return "ERROR";
        case LogLevel::Critical: return "CRIT ";
        default:                 return "?????";
    }
}

std::string Logger::levelToColor(LogLevel level) {
    switch (level) {
        case LogLevel::Trace:    return "\033[90m";      // Gray
        case LogLevel::Debug:    return "\033[36m";      // Cyan
        case LogLevel::Info:     return "\033[32m";      // Green
        case LogLevel::Warning:  return "\033[33m";      // Yellow
        case LogLevel::Error:    return "\033[31m";      // Red
        case LogLevel::Critical: return "\033[1;31m";    // Bold Red
        default:                 return "\033[0m";
    }
}

// Explicit template instantiations for common types
template std::string Logger::formatMessage(std::string_view, const char*);
template std::string Logger::formatMessage(std::string_view, std::string);
template std::string Logger::formatMessage(std::string_view, int);
template std::string Logger::formatMessage(std::string_view, float);
template std::string Logger::formatMessage(std::string_view, int, int);
template std::string Logger::formatMessage(std::string_view, const char*, int);
```
